## Findings & Recommendations
- A+/A win rate 34% vs B/C 38% -> grading NOT predictive this week - review PA grade criteria
- D-grade filter: filtered signals would have won 28% -> filter justified (<50%)
- 84% rule (Lesson 6 canonical 2026-07-06: solid B&R stop-out arms one re-entry on the reclaim close, ORIGINAL stop + target): 87 triggers, fired win rate 40%.
- 84% live wiring: armed per-symbol off paper stop-outs in live_scanner (2026-07-05). Requires --paper mode; signal-only runs have no stop-out feedback.
- Best setup: reentry_84_rule (40%) | worst: break_and_retest (37%)
- C-grade alerts (226, alert-only per SPEC2) would have won 31% - similar to traded grades; alert-only demotion costs little.
